# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-103">Routage dans ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-104">Par [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5), et [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-105">Routing est responsable de l’appariement des demandes HTTP entrantes et l’envoi de ces demandes aux paramètres exécutables de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-105">Routing is responsible for matching incoming HTTP requests and dispatching those requests to the app's executable endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-106">[Les points de terminaison](#endpoint) sont les unités de l’application de code exécutable de traitement des demandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-106">[Endpoints](#endpoint) are the app's units of executable request-handling code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-107">Les points de terminaison sont définis dans l’application et configurés lorsque l’application démarre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-107">Endpoints are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-108">Le processus de correspondance des points de terminaison peut extraire des valeurs de l’URL de la demande et fournir ces valeurs pour le traitement des demandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-108">The endpoint matching process can extract values from the request's URL and provide those values for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-109">En utilisant les informations de point de terminaison de l’application, le routage est également en mesure de générer des URL qui cartographient en points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-109">Using endpoint information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-110">Les applications peuvent configurer le routage à l’aide de :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-110">Apps can configure routing using:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="128d2-111">Controllers</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-111">Controllers</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="128d2-112">Pages Razor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-112">Razor Pages</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="128d2-113">SignalR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-113">SignalR</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="128d2-114">Services gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-114">gRPC Services</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="128d2-115">Middleware compatible avec le point de [terminaison](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) comme [les contrôles de santé](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-115">Endpoint-enabled [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) such as [Health Checks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="128d2-116">Délégués et lambdas inscrits avec itinéraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-116">Delegates and lambdas registered with routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-117">Ce document couvre les détails de bas niveau de ASP.NET itinéraire de base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-117">This document covers low-level details of ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-118">Pour plus d’informations sur le routage configuré :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-118">For information on configuring routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-119">Pour les contrôleurs, voir <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-119">For controllers, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-120">Pour les conventions <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>De Razor Pages, voir .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-120">For Razor Pages conventions, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-121">Le système de routage des points de terminaison décrit dans ce document s’applique à ASP.NET Core 3.0 et plus tard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-121">The endpoint routing system described in this document applies to ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-122">Pour plus d’informations sur <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>le système de routage précédent basé sur , sélectionnez la version ASP.NET Core 2.1 à l’aide d’une des approches suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-122">For information on the previous routing system based on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, select the ASP.NET Core 2.1 version using one of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-123">Le sélecteur de version pour une version précédente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-123">The version selector for a previous version.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-124">Sélectionnez [ASP.NET’itinéraire Core 2.1](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-124">Select [ASP.NET Core 2.1 routing](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-125">[Afficher ou télécharger le code de l’échantillon](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([comment télécharger](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-125">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-128">Concepts de base du routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-128">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-129">Tous les modèles ASP.NET Core incluent le routage dans le code généré.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-129">All ASP.NET Core templates include routing in the generated code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-130">Routing est enregistré dans le `Startup.Configure`pipeline [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) dans .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-130">Routing is registered in the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline in `Startup.Configure`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-131">Le code suivant montre un exemple de base de routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-131">The following code shows a basic example of routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet&highlight=8,10)]

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-132">Routing utilise une paire de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> middleware, enregistrée par et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-132">Routing uses a pair of middleware, registered by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-133">`UseRouting`ajoute l’appariement de l’itinéraire au pipeline middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-133">`UseRouting` adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-134">Ce middleware examine l’ensemble des points de terminaison définis dans l’application, et sélectionne le [meilleur match](#urlm) basé sur la demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-134">This middleware looks at the set of endpoints defined in the app, and selects the [best match](#urlm) based on the request.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-135">`UseEndpoints`ajoute l’exécution du point de terminaison au pipeline middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-135">`UseEndpoints` adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-136">Il exécute le délégué associé au critère de terminaison sélectionné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-136">It runs the delegate associated with the selected endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-137">L’exemple précédent comprend un itinéraire unique vers le point de terminaison *de code à* l’aide de la méthode [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-137">The preceding example includes a single *route to code* endpoint using the [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-138">Lorsqu’une `GET` demande HTTP est `/`envoyée à l’URL racine :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-138">When an HTTP `GET` request is sent to the root URL `/`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-139">Le délégué de demande montré exécute.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-139">The request delegate shown executes.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-140">`Hello World!`est écrit à la réponse HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-140">`Hello World!` is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-141">Par défaut, l’URL `/` racine est `https://localhost:5001/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-141">By default, the root URL `/` is `https://localhost:5001/`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-142">Si la méthode `GET` de demande n’est pas ou l’URL racine n’est pas `/`, aucun itinéraire ne correspond et un HTTP 404 est retourné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-142">If the request method is not `GET` or the root URL is not `/`, no route matches and an HTTP 404 is returned.</span></span>

### <a name="endpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-143">Point de terminaison</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-143">Endpoint</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-144">La `MapGet` méthode est utilisée pour définir un **critère d’évaluation**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-144">The `MapGet` method is used to define an **endpoint**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-145">Un point de terminaison est quelque chose qui peut être:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-145">An endpoint is something that can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-146">Sélectionné, en faisant correspondre l’URL et la méthode HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-146">Selected, by matching the URL and HTTP method.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-147">Exécuté, en exécutant le délégué.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-147">Executed, by running the delegate.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-148">Les points de terminaison qui peuvent être appariés et exécutés par l’application sont configurés dans `UseEndpoints`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-148">Endpoints that can be matched and executed by the app are configured in `UseEndpoints`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-149">Par <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>exemple, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, et [des méthodes similaires](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) relient les délégués de demande au système de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-149">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [similar methods](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connect request delegates to the routing system.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="128d2-150">D’autres méthodes peuvent être utilisées pour connecter ASP.NET fonctionnalités du cadre Core au système de routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-150">Additional methods can be used to connect ASP.NET Core framework features to the routing system:</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="128d2-151">MapRazorPages pour les pages Razor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-151">MapRazorPages for Razor Pages</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)
- [<span data-ttu-id="128d2-152">MapControllers pour les contrôleurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-152">MapControllers for controllers</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*)
- [<span data-ttu-id="128d2-153">MapHub\<THub> pour SignalR</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-153">MapHub\<THub> for SignalR</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="128d2-154">MapGrpcService\<TService> pour gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-154">MapGrpcService\<TService> for gRPC</span></span>](xref:grpc/aspnetcore)

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-155">L’exemple suivant montre l’itinéraire avec un modèle d’itinéraire plus sophistiqué :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-155">The following example shows routing with a more sophisticated route template:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-156">La `/hello/{name:alpha}` chaîne est un **modèle d’itinéraire**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-156">The string `/hello/{name:alpha}` is a **route template**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-157">Il est utilisé pour configurer la façon dont le point final est apparié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-157">It is used to configure how the endpoint is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-158">Dans ce cas, le modèle correspond à :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-158">In this case, the template matches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-159">Une URL comme`/hello/Ryan`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-159">A URL like `/hello/Ryan`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-160">Tout chemin URL `/hello/` qui commence par suivi d’une séquence de caractères alphabétiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-160">Any URL path that begins with `/hello/` followed by a sequence of alphabetic characters.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="128d2-161">`:alpha`applique une contrainte d’itinéraire qui ne correspond qu’aux caractères alphabétiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-161">`:alpha` applies a route constraint that matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-162">[Les contraintes d’itinéraire](#route-constraint-reference) sont expliquées plus tard dans ce document.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-162">[Route constraints](#route-constraint-reference) are explained later in this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-163">Le deuxième segment du `{name:alpha}`chemin URL, :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-163">The second segment of the URL path, `{name:alpha}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-164">Est lié `name` au paramètre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-164">Is bound to the `name` parameter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-165">Est capturé et stocké dans [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-165">Is captured and stored in [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-166">Le système de routage des points de terminaison décrit dans ce document est nouveau à partir de ASP.NET Core 3.0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-166">The endpoint routing system described in this document is new as of ASP.NET Core 3.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-167">Cependant, toutes les versions de ASP.NET Core prennent en charge le même ensemble de fonctionnalités de modèle d’itinéraire et de contraintes d’itinéraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-167">However, all versions of ASP.NET Core support the same set of route template features and route constraints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-169">L’exemple précédent montre comment :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-169">The preceding example demonstrates how:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-170">Le middleware d’autorisation peut être utilisé avec le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-170">The authorization middleware can be used with routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-171">Les points de terminaison peuvent être utilisés pour configurer le comportement d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-171">Endpoints can be used to configure authorization behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-172">L’appel <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> ajoute un point de terminaison de bilan de santé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-172">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> call adds a health check endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-173">L’enchaînement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> de cet appel attache une politique d’autorisation au point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-173">Chaining <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> on to this call attaches an authorization policy to the endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-174">Appeler <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> et ajouter l’authentification et l’autorisation middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-174">Calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> adds the authentication and authorization middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-175">Ces middleware sont <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> `UseEndpoints` placés entre et afin qu’ils puissent:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-175">These middleware are placed between <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and `UseEndpoints` so that they can:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-176">Voir quel critère d’évaluation a été choisi par `UseRouting`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-176">See which endpoint was selected by `UseRouting`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-177">Appliquer une politique <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> d’autorisation avant les envois au point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-177">Apply an authorization policy before <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> dispatches to the endpoint.</span></span>

<a name="metadata"></a>

### <a name="endpoint-metadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-178">Métadonnées de point de terminaison</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-178">Endpoint metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-179">Dans l’exemple précédent, il y a deux critères d’évaluation, mais seul le critère de vérification de santé comporte une politique d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-179">In the preceding example, there are two endpoints, but only the health check endpoint has an authorization policy attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-180">Si la demande correspond au `/healthz`critère de vérification de santé, une vérification d’autorisation est effectuée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-180">If the request matches the health check endpoint, `/healthz`, an authorization check is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-181">Cela démontre que les paramètres peuvent avoir des données supplémentaires qui leur sont rattachées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-181">This demonstrates that endpoints can have extra data attached to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-182">Ces données supplémentaires sont appelées **métadonnées**de point de terminaison :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-182">This extra data is called endpoint **metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-183">Les métadonnées peuvent être traitées par un moyen de restauration.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-183">The metadata can be processed by routing-aware middleware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-184">Les métadonnées peuvent être de n’importe quel type .NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-184">The metadata can be of any .NET type.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-185">Concepts de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-185">Routing concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-186">Le système de routage s’appuie sur le pipeline middleware en ajoutant le concept de **point de terminaison** puissant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-186">The routing system builds on top of the middleware pipeline by adding the powerful **endpoint** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-187">Les points de terminaison représentent des unités de fonctionnalités de l’application qui sont distinctes les unes des autres en termes de routage, d’autorisation et d’un certain nombre de systèmes ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-187">Endpoints represent units of the app's functionality that are distinct from each other in terms of routing, authorization, and any number of ASP.NET Core's systems.</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

### <a name="aspnet-core-endpoint-definition"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-188">définition ASP.NET point de terminaison de base</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-188">ASP.NET Core endpoint definition</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-189">Un critère d’évaluation ASP.NET Core est :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-189">An ASP.NET Core endpoint is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-190">Exécutable: <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>A un .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-190">Executable: Has a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-191">Extensible: A une collection [de métadonnées.](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-191">Extensible: Has a [Metadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-192">Sélection: Optionnellement, a [des informations de routage](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-192">Selectable: Optionally, has [routing information](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-193">Enumerable: La collecte des points de terminaison <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> peut être répertoriée en récupérant le de [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-193">Enumerable: The collection of endpoints can be listed by retrieving the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-212">Le `UseRouting` middleware utilise la méthode [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) pour attacher le point de terminaison au contexte actuel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-212">The `UseRouting` middleware uses the [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) method to attach the endpoint to the current context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-213">Il est possible de `UseRouting` remplacer le middleware par une logique personnalisée et encore obtenir les avantages de l’utilisation des points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-213">It's possible to replace the `UseRouting` middleware with custom logic and still get the benefits of using endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-214">Les points de terminaison sont un primitif de bas niveau comme middleware, et ne sont pas couplés à la mise en œuvre de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-214">Endpoints are a low-level primitive like middleware, and aren't coupled to the routing implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-215">La plupart des applications `UseRouting` n’ont pas besoin de remplacer par une logique personnalisée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-215">Most apps don't need to replace `UseRouting` with custom logic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-216">Le `UseEndpoints` middleware est conçu pour être `UseRouting` utilisé en tandem avec le middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-216">The `UseEndpoints` middleware is designed to be used in tandem with the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-217">La logique de base pour exécuter un point de terminaison n’est pas compliquée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-217">The core logic to execute an endpoint isn't complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-218">Utilisez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> pour récupérer le point de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> terminaison, puis invoquer sa propriété.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-218">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> to retrieve the endpoint, and then invoke its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> property.</span></span>

      * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-225">Inspecte habituellement les métadonnées pour comprendre les points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-225">Usually inspects metadata to understand the endpoints.</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-226">Prend souvent des décisions `UseAuthorization` de `UseCors`sécurité, comme cela se fait par et .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-226">Often makes security decisions, as done by `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>

### <a name="comparing-a-terminal-middleware-and-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-247">Comparaison d’un middleware terminal et d’un itinéraire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-247">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-248">L’échantillon de code suivant contraste à l’aide de middleware avec l’utilisation du routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-248">The following code sample contrasts using middleware with using routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/TerminalMiddlewareStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-249">Le style de middleware montré avec `Approach 1:` est terminal **middleware**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-249">The style of middleware shown with `Approach 1:` is **terminal middleware**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-250">C’est ce qu’on appelle le middleware terminal parce qu’il fait une opération de correspondance:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-250">It's called terminal middleware because it does a matching operation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-251">L’opération correspondante de `Path == "/"` l’échantillon précédent `Path == "/Movie"` est pour le middleware et pour le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-251">The matching operation in the preceding sample is `Path == "/"` for the middleware and `Path == "/Movie"` for routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-252">Quand un match est réussi, il exécute certaines fonctionnalités et `next` retourne, plutôt que d’invoquer le middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-252">When a match is successful, it executes some functionality and returns, rather than invoking the `next` middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-253">C’est ce qu’on appelle le middleware terminal parce qu’il met fin à la recherche, exécute certaines fonctionnalités, puis revient.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-253">It's called terminal middleware because it terminates the search, executes some functionality, and then returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-254">Comparaison d’un middleware terminal et d’un itinéraire :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-254">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-255">Les deux approches permettent de mettre fin au pipeline de traitement :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-255">Both approaches allow terminating the processing pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-256">Middleware met fin au pipeline en `next`revenant plutôt que d’invoquer .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-256">Middleware terminates the pipeline by returning rather than invoking `next`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-257">Les points de terminaison sont toujours terminaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-257">Endpoints are always terminal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-258">Terminal middleware permet de positionner le middleware à un endroit arbitraire dans le pipeline:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-258">Terminal middleware allows positioning the middleware at an arbitrary place in the pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-259">Les points de terminaison s’exécutent à la position de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-259">Endpoints execute at the position of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-260">Terminal middleware permet au code arbitraire de déterminer quand le middleware correspond:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-260">Terminal middleware allows arbitrary code to determine when the middleware matches:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-261">Le code d’appariement d’itinéraire personnalisé peut être verbeux et difficile à écrire correctement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-261">Custom route matching code can be verbose and difficult to write correctly.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-262">Routing fournit des solutions simples pour les applications typiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-262">Routing provides straightforward solutions for typical apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-263">La plupart des applications ne nécessitent pas de code d’appariement d’itinéraire personnalisé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-263">Most apps don't require custom route matching code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-264">Interface de point de terminaison avec middleware tels que `UseAuthorization` et `UseCors`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-264">Endpoints interface with middleware such as `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-265">L’utilisation d’un middleware terminal avec `UseAuthorization` ou `UseCors` nécessite un interfacrage manuel avec le système d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-265">Using a terminal middleware with `UseAuthorization` or `UseCors` requires manual interfacing with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-266">Un [point de terminaison](#endpoint) définit les deux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-266">An [endpoint](#endpoint) defines both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-267">Un délégué pour traiter les demandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-267">A delegate to process requests.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-268">Une collection de métadonnées arbitraires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-268">A collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-269">Les métadonnées sont utilisées pour mettre en œuvre des préoccupations transversales basées sur les politiques et la configuration fixées à chaque point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-269">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-270">Terminal middleware peut être un outil efficace, mais peut exiger:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-270">Terminal middleware can be an effective tool, but can require:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-271">Une quantité importante de codage et de tests.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-271">A significant amount of coding and testing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-272">Intégration manuelle avec d’autres systèmes pour atteindre le niveau de flexibilité souhaité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-272">Manual integration with other systems to achieve the desired level of flexibility.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-273">Envisagez de vous intégrer au routage avant d’écrire un middleware terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-273">Consider integrating with routing before writing a terminal middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-274">Middleware terminal existant qui s’intègre à [la carte](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) ou <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> peut généralement être transformé en un point de terminaison de routage conscient.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-274">Existing terminal middleware that integrates with [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> can usually be turned into a routing aware endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-275">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) montre le modèle pour routeur-ware:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-275">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) demonstrates the pattern for router-ware:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-276">Écrivez une <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>méthode d’extension sur .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-276">Write an extension method on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-277">Créez un pipeline de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder.CreateApplicationBuilder*>middleware imbriqué à l’aide de .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-277">Create a nested middleware pipeline using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder.CreateApplicationBuilder*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-278">Attachez le middleware au nouveau pipeline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-278">Attach the middleware to the new pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-279">Dans ce cas, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-279">In this case, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*>le pipeline middleware <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>dans un .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-280"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*> the middleware pipeline into a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-281">Appelez `Map` et fournissez le nouveau pipeline middleware.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-281">Call `Map` and provide the new middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-282">Retournez l’objet `Map` constructeur fourni par la méthode d’extension.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-282">Return the builder object provided by `Map` from the extension method.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-283">Le code suivant montre l’utilisation de [MapHealthChecks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-283">The following code shows use of [MapHealthChecks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-284">L’échantillon précédent montre pourquoi le retour de l’objet constructeur est important.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-284">The preceding sample shows why returning the builder object is important.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-285">Le retour de l’objet constructeur permet au développeur d’applications de configurer des stratégies telles que l’autorisation pour le point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-285">Returning the builder object allows the app developer to configure policies such as authorization for the endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-286">Dans cet exemple, les contrôles de santé middleware n’a pas d’intégration directe avec le système d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-286">In this example, the health checks middleware has no direct integration with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-287">Le système de métadonnées a été créé en réponse aux problèmes rencontrés par les auteurs d’extéabilité à l’aide de middleware terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-287">The metadata system was created in response to the problems encountered by extensibility authors using terminal middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-288">Il est problématique pour chaque middleware de mettre en œuvre sa propre intégration avec le système d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-288">It's problematic for each middleware to implement its own integration with the authorization system.</span></span>

<a name="urlm"></a>

### <a name="url-matching"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-289">Correspondance d’URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-289">URL matching</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-290">Est le processus par lequel l’itinéraire correspond à une demande entrante à un [point de terminaison](#endpoint).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-290">Is the process by which routing matches an incoming request to an [endpoint](#endpoint).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-291">Est basé sur les données dans le chemin DE l’URL et les en-têtes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-291">Is based on data in the URL path and headers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-292">Peut être étendu pour tenir compte de toutes les données de la demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-292">Can be extended to consider any data in the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-293">Lorsqu’un middleware de routage `Endpoint` s’exécute, il définit <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> une valeur et l’itinéraire à une fonction de [demande](xref:fundamentals/request-features) sur la demande actuelle :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-293">When a routing middleware executes, it sets an `Endpoint` and route values to a [request feature](xref:fundamentals/request-features) on the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpContext> from the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-294">Appeler [HttpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) obtient le point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-294">Calling [HttpContext.GetEndpoint](<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*>) gets the endpoint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-295">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` récupère la collection de valeurs d’itinéraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-295">`HttpRequest.RouteValues` gets the collection of route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-296">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) en cours d’exécution après le middleware routage peut inspecter le point de terminaison et prendre des mesures.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-296">[Middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) running after the routing middleware can inspect the endpoint and take action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-297">Par exemple, un middleware d’autorisation peut interroger la collecte des métadonnées du point final pour une politique d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-297">For example, an authorization middleware can interrogate the endpoint's metadata collection for an authorization policy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-298">Une fois que tous les intergiciels dans le pipeline de traitement de requêtes sont exécutés, le délégué du point de terminaison sélectionné est appelé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-298">After all of the middleware in the request processing pipeline is executed, the selected endpoint's delegate is invoked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-299">Le système de routage dans le routage de point de terminaison est responsable de toutes les décisions de distribution.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-299">The routing system in endpoint routing is responsible for all dispatching decisions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-300">Étant donné que le middleware applique des stratégies basées sur le critère d’évaluation sélectionné, il est important que :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-300">Because the middleware applies policies based on the selected endpoint, it's important that:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-301">Toute décision qui peut affecter l’expédition ou l’application des politiques de sécurité est prise à l’intérieur du système de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-301">Any decision that can affect dispatching or the application of security policies is made inside the routing system.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-302">Pour la compatibilité à l’envers, lorsqu’un délégué de point de terminaison Controller ou Razor Pages est exécuté, les propriétés de [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) sont définies à des valeurs appropriées en fonction du traitement de demande effectué jusqu’à présent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-302">For backwards-compatibility, when a Controller or Razor Pages endpoint delegate is executed, the properties of [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) are set to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-303">Le `RouteContext` type sera marqué obsolète dans une prochaine version:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-303">The `RouteContext` type will be marked obsolete in a future release:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-304">Migrer `RouteData.Values` vers `HttpRequest.RouteValues`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-304">Migrate `RouteData.Values` to `HttpRequest.RouteValues`.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-305">Migrez `RouteData.DataTokens` pour récupérer [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) à partir des métadonnées de point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-305">Migrate `RouteData.DataTokens` to retrieve [IDataTokensMetadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IDataTokensMetadata) from the endpoint metadata.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-306">L’appariement d’URL fonctionne dans un ensemble configurable de phases.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-306">URL matching operates in a configurable set of phases.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-307">Dans chaque phase, la sortie est un ensemble de correspondances.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-307">In each phase, the output is a set of matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-308">L’ensemble des matchs peut être réduit davantage par la phase suivante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-308">The set of matches can be narrowed down further by the next phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-309">La mise en œuvre de routage ne garantit pas une commande de traitement pour l’appariement des points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-309">The routing implementation does not guarantee a processing order for matching endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-310">**Tous les** correspondances possibles sont traitées à la fois.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-310">**All** possible matches are processed at once.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-311">Les phases de correspondance de l’URL se produisent dans l’ordre suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-311">The URL matching phases occur in the following order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-312">ASP.NET Core :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-312">ASP.NET Core:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="128d2-313">Traite le chemin URL par rapport à l’ensemble des points de terminaison et de leurs modèles d’itinéraire, en recueillant **tous les** matchs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-313">Processes the URL path against the set of endpoints and their route templates, collecting **all** of the matches.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="128d2-314">Prend la liste précédente et supprime les correspondances qui échouent avec des contraintes d’itinéraire appliquées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-314">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail with route constraints applied.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="128d2-315">Prend la liste précédente et supprime les correspondances qui échouent à l’ensemble des instances [MatcherPolicy.](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-315">Takes the preceding list and removes matches that fail the set of [MatcherPolicy](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.MatcherPolicy) instances.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="128d2-316">Utilise [l’outil d’évaluationSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) pour prendre une décision finale de la liste précédente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-316">Uses the [EndpointSelector](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector) to make a final decision from the preceding list.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-317">La liste des critères d’évaluation est priorisée en fonction des critères :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-317">The list of endpoints is prioritized according to:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-318">Le [RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-318">The [RouteEndpoint.Order](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order*)</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-319">La [préséance du modèle d’itinéraire](#rtp)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-319">The [route template precedence](#rtp)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-320">Tous les critères d’évaluation correspondants sont traités dans chaque phase jusqu’à ce que le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector> soit atteint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-320">All matching endpoints are processed in each phase until the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Matching.EndpointSelector> is reached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-321">C’est `EndpointSelector` la phase finale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-321">The `EndpointSelector` is the final phase.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-322">Il choisit le point de terminaison la plus prioritaire des matchs comme meilleur match.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-322">It chooses the highest priority endpoint from the matches as the best match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-323">S’il y a d’autres matchs avec la même priorité que le meilleur match, une exception de match ambigue est lancée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-323">If there are other matches with the same priority as the best match, an ambiguous match exception is thrown.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-324">La préséance de l’itinéraire est calculée sur la base d’un modèle d’itinéraire **plus spécifique** étant donné une priorité plus élevée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-324">The route precedence is computed based on a **more specific** route template being given a higher priority.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-325">Par exemple, considérez `/hello` `/{message}`les modèles et :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-325">For example, consider the templates `/hello` and `/{message}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-326">Les deux correspondent `/hello`au chemin URL .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-326">Both match the URL path `/hello`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-327">`/hello`est plus spécifique et donc une priorité plus élevée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-327">`/hello`  is more specific and therefore higher priority.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-328">En général, la préséance de route fait un bon travail de choisir le meilleur match pour les types de systèmes d’URL utilisés dans la pratique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-328">In general, route precedence does a good job of choosing the best match for the kinds of URL schemes used in practice.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-329">Utiliser <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> uniquement si nécessaire pour éviter une ambiguïté.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-329">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.Order> only when necessary to avoid an ambiguity.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-330">En raison des types d’extéabilité fourni par le routage, il n’est pas possible pour le système de routage de calculer à l’avance les itinéraires ambigus.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-330">Due to the kinds of extensibility provided by routing, it isn't possible for the routing system to compute ahead of time the ambiguous routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-331">Prenons un exemple tel que `/{message:alpha}` `/{message:int}`les modèles d’itinéraire et :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-331">Consider an example such as the route templates `/{message:alpha}` and `/{message:int}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-332">La `alpha` contrainte ne correspond qu’aux caractères alphabétiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-332">The `alpha` constraint matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-333">La `int` contrainte ne correspond qu’aux nombres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-333">The `int` constraint matches only numbers.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-334">Ces modèles ont la même priorité d’itinéraire, mais il n’y a pas d’URL unique qu’ils correspondent tous les deux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-334">These templates have the same route precedence, but there's no single URL they both match.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-335">Si le système de routage a signalé une erreur d’ambiguïté au démarrage, il bloquerait ce cas d’utilisation valide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-335">If the routing system reported an ambiguity error at startup, it would block this valid use case.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
>
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-336">L’ordre des <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> opérations à l’intérieur n’influence pas le comportement du routage, à une exception près.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-336">The order of operations inside <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> doesn't influence the behavior of routing, with one exception.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-337"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*>et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> attribuez automatiquement une valeur de commande à leurs points de terminaison en fonction de l’ordre qu’ils sont invoqués.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-337"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllerRoute*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MvcAreaRouteBuilderExtensions.MapAreaRoute*> automatically assign an order value to their endpoints based on the order they are invoked.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-338">Cela simule le comportement à long terme des contrôleurs sans le système de routage fournissant les mêmes garanties que les anciennes implémentations de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-338">This simulates long-time behavior of controllers without the routing system providing the same guarantees as older routing implementations.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-339">Dans la mise en œuvre héritée du routage, il est possible de mettre en œuvre l’extensibility de routage qui dépend de l’ordre dans lequel les itinéraires sont traités.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-339">In the legacy implementation of routing, it's possible to implement routing extensibility that has a dependency on the order in which routes are processed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-340">Itinéraire de point de terminaison dans ASP.NET Core 3.0 et plus tard :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-340">Endpoint routing in ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later:</span></span>
> 
> * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-341">N’a pas de concept d’itinéraires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-341">Doesn't have a concept of routes.</span></span>
> * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-342">Ne fournit pas de garanties de commande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-342">Doesn't provide ordering guarantees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-343">Tous les critères d’évaluation sont traités à la fois.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-343">All endpoints are processed at once.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-344">Si cela signifie que vous êtes coincé à l’aide du système de routage hérité, [ouvrez un problème GitHub pour obtenir de l’aide](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-344">If this means you're stuck using the legacy routing system, [open a GitHub issue for assistance](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/issues).</span></span>

<a name="rtp"></a>

### <a name="route-template-precedence-and-endpoint-selection-order"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-345">Priorité du modèle d’itinéraire et ordre de sélection des points de terminaison</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-345">Route template precedence and endpoint selection order</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-346">[La préséance du modèle d’itinéraire](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) est un système qui attribue à chaque modèle d’itinéraire une valeur basée sur sa spécificité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-346">[Route template precedence](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L16) is a system that assigns each route template a value based on how specific it is.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-347">Priorité du modèle d’itinéraire :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-347">Route template precedence:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-348">Évite la nécessité d’ajuster l’ordre des points de terminaison dans les cas courants.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-348">Avoids the need to adjust the order of endpoints in common cases.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-349">Tentatives pour correspondre aux attentes de bon sens du comportement de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-349">Attempts to match the common-sense expectations of routing behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-350">Par exemple, considérez les `/Products/List` modèles et `/Products/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-350">For example, consider templates `/Products/List` and `/Products/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-351">Il serait raisonnable de `/Products/List` supposer que `/Products/{id}` c’est `/Products/List`un meilleur match que pour le chemin URL .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-351">It would be reasonable to assume that `/Products/List` is a better match than `/Products/{id}` for the URL path `/Products/List`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-352">Les œuvres parce `/List` que le segment littéral `/{id}`est considéré comme ayant une meilleure préséance que le segment des paramètres .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-352">The works because the literal segment `/List` is considered to have better precedence than the parameter segment `/{id}`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-353">Les détails du fonctionnement de la préséance sont couplés à la façon dont les modèles d’itinéraire sont définis :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-353">The details of how precedence works are coupled to how route templates are defined:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-354">Les modèles avec plus de segments sont considérés comme plus spécifiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-354">Templates with more segments are considered more specific.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-355">Un segment avec du texte littéral est considéré comme plus spécifique qu’un segment de paramètres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-355">A segment with literal text is considered more specific than a parameter segment.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-356">Un segment de paramètre avec une contrainte est considéré comme plus spécifique qu’un sans.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-356">A parameter segment with a constraint is considered more specific than one without.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-357">Un segment complexe est considéré comme spécifique comme un segment de paramètres avec une contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-357">A complex segment is considered as specific as a parameter segment with a constraint.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-358">Attraper tous les paramètres sont les moins spécifiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-358">Catch all parameters are the least specific.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-359">Voir le [code source sur GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) pour une référence des valeurs exactes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-359">See the [source code on GitHub](https://github.com/dotnet/aspnetcore/blob/master/src/Http/Routing/src/Template/RoutePrecedence.cs#L189) for a reference of exact values.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-360">Concepts de génération d’URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-360">URL generation concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-361">Génération d’URL :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-361">URL generation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-362">Est-ce le processus par lequel le routage peut créer un chemin URL basé sur un ensemble de valeurs d’itinéraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-362">Is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="128d2-363">Permet une séparation logique entre les points de terminaison et les URL qui y accèdent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-363">Allows for a logical separation between endpoints and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-364">Le routage des <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> points de terminaison comprend l’API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-364">Endpoint routing includes the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-365">`LinkGenerator`est un service singleton disponible à partir de [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-365">`LinkGenerator` is a singleton service available from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-366">L’API `LinkGenerator` peut être utilisée en dehors du contexte d’une demande d’exécution.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-366">The `LinkGenerator` API can be used outside of the context of an executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) et les scénarios <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>qui s’appuient sur , tels que Tag `LinkGenerator` [Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, et Résultats [d’action](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), utiliser l’API en interne pour fournir des capacités de génération de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-367">[Mvc.IUrlHelper](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper) and scenarios that rely on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.IUrlHelper>, such as [Tag Helpers](xref:mvc/views/tag-helpers/intro), HTML Helpers, and [Action Results](xref:mvc/controllers/actions), use the `LinkGenerator` API internally to provide link generating capabilities.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-368">Le générateur de liens est basé sur le concept d’une **adresse** et de **schémas d’adresse**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-368">The link generator is backed by the concept of an **address** and **address schemes**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-369">Un schéma d’adresse est un moyen de déterminer les points de terminaison à prendre en compte pour la génération de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-369">An address scheme is a way of determining the endpoints that should be considered for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-370">Par exemple, les scénarios de noms d’itinéraire et de valeurs d’itinéraire que beaucoup d’utilisateurs connaissent des contrôleurs et les pages Razor sont implémentées comme un schéma d’adresse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-370">For example, the route name and route values scenarios many users are familiar with from controllers and Razor Pages are implemented as an address scheme.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-371">Le générateur de liaison peut être relié aux contrôleurs et aux pages Razor via les méthodes d’extension suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-371">The link generator can link to controllers and Razor Pages via the following extension methods:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.ControllerLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByAction*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetPathByPage*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.PageLinkGeneratorExtensions.GetUriByPage*>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-372">Les surcharges de ces méthodes `HttpContext`acceptent les arguments qui incluent le .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-372">Overloads of these methods accept arguments that include the `HttpContext`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-373">Ces méthodes sont fonctionnellement équivalentes à [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) et [Url.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*), mais offrent une flexibilité et des options supplémentaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-373">These methods are functionally equivalent to [Url.Action](xref:System.Web.Mvc.UrlHelper.Action*) and [Url.Page](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.UrlHelperExtensions.Page*), but offer additional flexibility and options.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-374">Les `GetPath*` méthodes sont `Url.Action` plus `Url.Page`similaires et, en ce qu’elles génèrent un URI contenant un chemin absolu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-374">The `GetPath*` methods are most similar to `Url.Action` and `Url.Page`, in that they generate a URI containing an absolute path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-375">Les méthodes `GetUri*` génèrent toujours un URI absolu contenant un schéma et un hôte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-375">The `GetUri*` methods always generate an absolute URI containing a scheme and host.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-376">Les méthodes qui acceptent un `HttpContext` génèrent un URI dans le contexte de la requête en cours d’exécution.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-376">The methods that accept an `HttpContext` generate a URI in the context of the executing request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-377">Les valeurs [de l’itinéraire ambiant,](#ambient) le chemin de base de l’URL, le schéma et l’hôte de la demande d’exécution sont utilisés à moins d’être dépassés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-377">The [ambient](#ambient) route values, URL base path, scheme, and host from the executing request are used unless overridden.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> est appelé avec une adresse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-378"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> is called with an address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-379">La génération d’un URI se fait en deux étapes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-379">Generating a URI occurs in two steps:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="128d2-380">Une adresse est liée à une liste de points de terminaison qui correspondent à l’adresse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-380">An address is bound to a list of endpoints that match the address.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="128d2-381">Le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> de chaque point de terminaison est évalué jusqu’à ce qu’un modèle de route correspondant aux valeurs fournies soit trouvé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-381">Each endpoint's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern> is evaluated until a route pattern that matches the supplied values is found.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-382">Le résultat obtenu est combiné avec d’autres parties de l’URI fournies par le générateur de liens, puis il est retourné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-382">The resulting output is combined with the other URI parts supplied to the link generator and returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-383">Les méthodes fournies par <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> prennent en charge des fonctionnalités de génération de liens standard pour n’importe quel type d’adresse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-383">The methods provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> support standard link generation capabilities for any type of address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-384">La façon la plus pratique d’utiliser le générateur de lien est par des méthodes d’extension qui effectuent des opérations pour un type d’adresse spécifique:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-384">The most convenient way to use the link generator is through extension methods that perform operations for a specific address type:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-385">Méthode d'extension</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-385">Extension Method</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-386">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-386">Description</span></span> |
| ---------------- | ----------- |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetPathByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-387">Génère un URI avec un chemin absolu basé sur les valeurs fournies.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-387">Generates a URI with an absolute path based on the provided values.</span></span> |
| <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator.GetUriByAddress*> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-388">Génère un URI absolu basé sur les valeurs fournies.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-388">Generates an absolute URI based on the provided values.</span></span>             |

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-389">Faites attention aux implications suivantes de l’appel de méthodes <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-389">Pay attention to the following implications of calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> methods:</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-390">Utilisez les méthodes d’extension `GetUri*` avec précaution dans une configuration d’application qui ne valide pas l’en-tête `Host` des requêtes entrantes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-390">Use `GetUri*` extension methods with caution in an app configuration that doesn't validate the `Host` header of incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-391">Si `Host` l’en-tête des demandes entrantes n’est pas validé, l’entrée de demande non fiable peut être renvoyée au client dans les URL dans une vue ou une page.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-391">If the `Host` header of incoming requests isn't validated, untrusted request input can be sent back to the client in URIs in a view or page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-392">Nous recommandons que toutes les applications de production configurent leur serveur pour qu’il valide l’en-tête `Host` par rapport à des valeurs valides connues.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-392">We recommend that all production apps configure their server to validate the `Host` header against known valid values.</span></span>
>
> * <span data-ttu-id="128d2-393">Utilisez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> avec précaution dans le middleware en combinaison avec `Map` ou `MapWhen`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-393">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> with caution in middleware in combination with `Map` or `MapWhen`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-394">`Map*` modifie le chemin de base de la requête en cours d’exécution, ce qui affecte la sortie de la génération de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-394">`Map*` changes the base path of the executing request, which affects the output of link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-395">Toutes les API <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> permettent la spécification d’un chemin de base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-395">All of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> APIs allow specifying a base path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-396">Spécifier un chemin `Map*` de base vide pour annuler l’effet sur la génération de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-396">Specify an empty base path to undo the `Map*` affect on link generation.</span></span>

### <a name="middleware-example"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-397">Exemple de middleware</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-397">Middleware example</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-398">Dans l’exemple suivant, un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> middleware utilise l’API pour créer un lien vers une méthode d’action qui répertorie les produits de stockage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-398">In the following example, a middleware uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.LinkGenerator> API to create a link to an action method that lists store products.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-399">L’utilisation du générateur de lien en `GenerateLink` l’injectant dans une classe et l’appel est disponible pour n’importe quelle classe dans une application :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-399">Using the link generator by injecting it into a class and calling `GenerateLink` is available to any class in an app:</span></span>
