<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1460">Le tableau suivant montre les réponses avec les URI donnés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1460">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1461">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1461">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1462">response</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1462">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1463">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1463">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1464">Valeurs de route : [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1464">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1465">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1465">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1466">Valeurs de route : [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1466">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1467">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1467">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1468">Valeurs de route : [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1468">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1469">La requête passe à travers ceci, aucune correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1469">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1470">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1470">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1471">La requête passe à travers ceci, correspondance seulement avec HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1471">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1472">La requête passe à travers ceci, aucune correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1472">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1473">Si vous configurez une seule route, appelez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> en passant une instance `IRouter`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1473">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1474">Vous n’avez pas besoin d’utiliser <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1474">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1475">Le framework fournit un ensemble de méthodes d’extension pour la création de routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1475">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1476">Certaines des méthodes listées, comme <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, nécessitent un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1476">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1477"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> est utilisé comme *gestionnaire de routage* quand une correspondance est trouvée pour la route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1477">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1478">D’autres méthodes de cette famille permettent de configurer un pipeline de middleware utilisé comme gestionnaire de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1478">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1479">Si la méthode `Map*` n’accepte pas de gestionnaire, comme <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, elle utilise le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1479">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1480">Les méthodes `Map[Verb]` utilisent des contraintes pour limiter la route au verbe HTTP dans le nom de la méthode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1480">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1481">Par exemple, consultez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1481">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-1482">Informations de référence sur les modèles de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1482">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1483">Les jetons placés entre accolades (`{ ... }`) définissent des *paramètres de routage* qui sont liés si une correspondance est trouvée pour la route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1483">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1484">Vous pouvez définir plusieurs paramètres de routage dans un segment de route, mais ils doivent être séparés par une valeur littérale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1484">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1485">Par exemple `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` n’est pas une route valide, car il n’y a aucune valeur littérale entre `{controller}` et `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1485">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1486">Ces paramètres de routage doivent avoir un nom, et ils autorisent la spécification d’attributs supplémentaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1486">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1487">Un texte littéral autre que les paramètres de routage (par exemple, `{id}`) et le séparateur de chemin `/` doit correspondre au texte présent dans l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1487">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1488">La correspondance de texte ne respecte pas la casse et est basée sur la représentation décodée du chemin des URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1488">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1489">Pour mettre en correspondance un délimiteur de paramètre de route littéral (`{` ou `}`), placez-le dans une séquence d’échappement en répétant le caractère (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1489">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1490">Les modèles d’URL qui tentent de capturer un nom de fichier avec une extension de fichier facultative doivent faire l’objet de considérations supplémentaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1490">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1491">Prenez par exemple le modèle `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1491">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1492">Quand des valeurs existent à la fois pour `filename` et pour `ext`, les deux valeurs sont renseignées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1492">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1493">Si seule une valeur existe pour `filename` dans l’URL, une correspondance est trouvée pour la route, car le point final (`.`) est facultatif.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1493">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1494">Les URL suivantes correspondent à cette route :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1494">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1495">Vous pouvez utiliser l’astérisque (`*`) comme préfixe d’un paramètre de route à lier au reste de l’URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1495">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1496">Cela s’appelle un paramètre *fourre-tout*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1496">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1497">Par exemple, `blog/{*slug}` établit une correspondance avec n’importe quel URI commençant par `/blog` et suivi de n’importe quelle valeur, qui est affectée à la valeur de route `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1497">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1498">Les paramètres fourre-tout peuvent également établir une correspondance avec la chaîne vide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1498">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1499">Le paramètre fourre-tout place les caractères appropriés dans une séquence d’échappement lorsque la route est utilisée pour générer une URL, y compris les caractères de séparation de chemin (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1499">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1500">Par exemple, la route `foo/{*path}` avec les valeurs de route `{ path = "my/path" }` génère `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1500">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1501">Notez la barre oblique d’échappement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1501">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1502">Les paramètres de route peuvent avoir des *valeurs par défaut*, désignées en spécifiant la valeur par défaut après le nom du paramètre, séparée par un signe égal (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1502">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1503">Par exemple, `{controller=Home}` définit `Home` comme valeur par défaut de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1503">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1504">La valeur par défaut est utilisée si aucune valeur n’est présente dans l’URL pour le paramètre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1504">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1505">Vous pouvez rendre facultatifs les paramètres de route en ajoutant un point d’interrogation (`?`) à la fin du nom du paramètre, comme dans `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1505">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1506">La différence entre les valeurs facultatives et les paramètres de route par défaut est qu’un paramètre de route ayant une valeur par défaut produit toujours une valeur, tandis qu’un paramètre facultatif a une valeur seulement quand celle-ci est fournie par l’URL de requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1506">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1507">Les paramètres de route peuvent avoir des contraintes, qui doivent correspondre à la valeur de route liée à partir de l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1507">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1508">L’ajout d’un signe deux-points (`:`) et d’un nom de contrainte après le nom du paramètre de routage spécifie une *contrainte inline* sur un paramètre de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1508">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1509">Si la contrainte nécessite des arguments, ils sont fournis entre parenthèses (`(...)`) après le nom de la contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1509">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1510">Il est possible de spécifier plusieurs contraintes inline en ajoutant un autre signe deux-points (`:`) et le nom d’une autre contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1510">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1511">Le nom de la contrainte et les arguments sont passés au service <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> pour créer une instance de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> à utiliser dans le traitement des URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1511">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1512">Par exemple, le modèle de routage `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` spécifie une contrainte `minlength` avec l’argument `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1512">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1513">Pour plus d’informations sur les contraintes de route et pour obtenir la liste des contraintes fournies par le framework, consultez la section [Informations de référence sur les contraintes de route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1513">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1514">Le tableau suivant montre des exemples de modèles de route et leur comportement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1514">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1515">Modèle de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1515">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1516">Exemple d’URI en correspondance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1516">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1517">URI de la requête&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1517">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1518">Correspond seulement au chemin unique `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1518">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1519">Correspond à `Page` et le définit sur `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1519">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1520">Correspond à `Page` et le définit sur `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1520">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1521">Mappe au contrôleur `Products` et à l’action `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1521">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1522">Mappe au contrôleur `Products` et à l’action `Details` (`id` défini sur 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1522">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1523">Mappe au contrôleur `Home` et à la méthode `Index` (`id` est ignoré).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1523">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1524">L’utilisation d’un modèle est généralement l’approche la plus simple pour le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1524">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1525">Il est également possible de spécifier des contraintes et des valeurs par défaut hors du modèle de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1525">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1526">Activez la [journalisation](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pour voir comment les implémentations de routage intégrées, comme <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, établissent des correspondances avec les requêtes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1526">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-1527">Informations de référence sur les contraintes de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1527">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1528">Les contraintes de route s’exécutent quand une correspondance s’est produite pour l’URL entrante, et le chemin de l’URL est tokenisé en valeurs de route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1528">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1529">En général, les contraintes de routage inspectent la valeur de route associée par le biais du modèle de routage, et créent une décision oui/non indiquant si la valeur est, ou non, acceptable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1529">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1530">Certaines contraintes de routage utilisent des données hors de la valeur de route pour déterminer si la requête peut être routée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1530">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1531">Par exemple, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> peut accepter ou rejeter une requête en fonction de son verbe HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1531">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1532">Les contraintes sont utilisées dans le routage des requêtes et la génération des liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1532">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1533">N’utilisez pas de contraintes pour la **validation des entrées**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1533">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1534">Si des contraintes sont utilisées pour la **validation des entrées**, une entrée non valide génère une réponse *404 - Introuvable* au lieu d’une réponse *400 - Requête incorrecte* avec un message d’erreur approprié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1534">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1535">Les contraintes de route sont utilisées pour **lever l’ambiguïté** entre des routes similaires, et non pas pour valider les entrées d’une route particulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1535">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1536">Le tableau suivant montre des exemples de contrainte de route et leur comportement attendu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1536">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1537">contrainte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1537">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1538">Exemple</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1538">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1539">Exemples de correspondances</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1539">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1540">Notes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1540">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1541">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1541">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1542">Correspond à n’importe quel entier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1542">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1543">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1543">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1544">Correspond à `true` ou à `false` (non-respect de la casse)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1544">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1545">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1545">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1546">Correspond à `DateTime` une valeur valable dans la culture invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1546">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1547">Voir l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1547">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1548">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1548">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1549">Correspond à `decimal` une valeur valable dans la culture invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1549">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1550">Voir l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1550">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1551">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1551">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1552">Correspond à `double` une valeur valable dans la culture invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1552">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1553">Voir l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1553">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1554">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1554">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1555">Correspond à `float` une valeur valable dans la culture invariante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1555">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1556">Voir l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1556">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1557">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1557">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1558">Correspond à une valeur `Guid` valide</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1558">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1559">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1559">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1560">Correspond à une valeur `long` valide</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1560">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1561">La chaîne doit comporter au moins 4 caractères</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1561">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1562">La chaîne ne doit pas comporter plus de 8 caractères</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1562">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1563">La chaîne doit comporter exactement 12 caractères</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1563">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1564">La chaîne doit comporter au moins 8 caractères et pas plus de 16 caractères</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1564">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1565">La valeur entière doit être au moins égale à 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1565">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1566">La valeur entière ne doit pas être supérieure à 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1566">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1567">La valeur entière doit être au moins égale à 18 mais ne doit pas être supérieure à 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1567">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1568">La chaîne doit se composer d’un ou de plusieurs caractères alphabétiques (`a`-`z`, non-respect de la casse)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1568">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1569">La chaîne doit correspondre à l’expression régulière (voir les conseils relatifs à la définition d’une expression régulière)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1569">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1570">Utilisé pour garantir qu’une valeur autre qu’un paramètre est présente pendant la génération de l’URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1570">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1571">Il est possible d’appliquer plusieurs contraintes séparées par un point-virgule à un même paramètre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1571">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1572">Par exemple, la contrainte suivante limite un paramètre à une valeur entière supérieure ou égale à 1 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1572">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1573">Les contraintes de routage qui vérifient que l’URL peut être convertie en type CLR (comme `int` ou `DateTime`) utilisent toujours la culture invariant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1573">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1574">ces contraintes partent du principe que l’URL n’est pas localisable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1574">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1575">Les contraintes de routage fournies par le framework ne modifient pas les valeurs stockées dans les valeurs de route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1575">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1576">Toutes les valeurs de route analysées à partir de l’URL sont stockées sous forme de chaînes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1576">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1577">Par exemple, la contrainte `float` tente de convertir la valeur de route en valeur float, mais la valeur convertie est utilisée uniquement pour vérifier qu’elle peut être convertie en valeur float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1577">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-1578">Expressions régulières</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1578">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1579">Le framework ASP.NET Core ajoute `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` au constructeur d’expression régulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1579">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1580">Pour obtenir une description de ces membres, consultez <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1580">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1581">Les expressions régulières utilisent les délimiteurs et des jetons semblables à ceux utilisés par le service de routage et le langage C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1581">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1582">Les jetons d’expression régulière doivent être placés dans une séquence d’échappement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1582">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1583">Pour que l’expression régulière `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` puisse être utilisée dans le routage, il faut que les caractères `\` (une seule barre oblique inverse) soit fournis dans la chaîne sous la forme `\\` (double barre oblique inverse) dans le fichier source C#, pour placer en échappement le caractère d’échappement de chaîne `\` (sauf en cas d’utilisation de [littéraux de chaîne textuelle](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1583">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1584">Pour placer en échappement les caractères de délimiteur de paramètre de route (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), doublez les caractères dans l’expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1584">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1585">Le tableau suivant montre une expression régulière et la version placée en échappement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1585">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1586">Expression régulière</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1586">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1587">Expression régulière en échappement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1587">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1588">Les expressions régulières utilisées dans le routage commencent souvent par un caret (`^`) et correspondent à la position de début de la chaîne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1588">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1589">Les expressions se terminent souvent par le signe dollar (`$`) de caractère et correspondent à la fin de la chaîne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1589">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1590">Les caractères `^` et `$` garantissent que l’expression régulière établit une correspondance avec la totalité de la valeur du paramètre de route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1590">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1591">Sans les caractères `^` et `$`, l’expression régulière peut correspondre à n’importe quelle sous-chaîne dans la chaîne, ce qui est souvent indésirable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1591">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1592">Le tableau suivant contient des exemples et explique pourquoi ils établissent ou non une correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1592">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1593">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1593">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1594">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1594">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1595">Correspond</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1595">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1596">Commentaire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1596">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1597">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1597">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1598">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1598">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1599">Correspondances de sous-chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1599">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1600">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1600">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1601">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1601">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1602">Correspondances de sous-chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1602">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1603">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1603">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1604">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1604">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1605">Correspondance avec l’expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1605">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1606">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1606">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1607">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1607">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1608">Non-respect de la casse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1608">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1609">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1609">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1610">Non</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1610">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1611">Voir `^` et `$` ci-dessus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1611">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1612">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1612">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1613">Non</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1613">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1614">Voir `^` et `$` ci-dessus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1614">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1615">Pour plus d’informations sur la syntaxe des expressions régulières, consultez [Expressions régulières du .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1615">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1616">Pour contraindre un paramètre à un ensemble connu de valeurs possibles, utilisez une expression régulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1616">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1617">Par exemple, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` établit une correspondance avec la valeur de route `action` uniquement pour `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1617">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1618">Si elle est passée dans le dictionnaire de contraintes, la chaîne `^(list|get|create)$` est équivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1618">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1619">Les contraintes passées dans le dictionnaire de contraintes (c’est-à-dire qui ne sont pas inline dans un modèle) qui ne correspondent pas à l’une des contraintes connues sont également traitées comme des expressions régulières.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1619">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-1620">Contraintes d’itinéraire personnalisé</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1620">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1621">Outre les contraintes d’itinéraire intégré, les contraintes d’itinéraire personnalisé peuvent être créées en implémentant l’interface <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1621">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1622">L’interface <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contient une méthode unique, `Match`, qui retourne `true` si la contrainte est satisfaite et `false` dans le cas contraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1622">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1623">Pour utiliser un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personnalisé, le type de contrainte d’itinéraire doit être inscrit avec le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> de l’application dans le conteneur de service de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1623">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1624">Un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> est un dictionnaire qui mappe les clés de contrainte d’itinéraire aux implémentations <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> qui valident ces contraintes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1624">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1625">Le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> d’une application peut être mis à jour dans `Startup.ConfigureServices` dans le cadre d’un appel [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou en configurant <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directement avec `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1625">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1626">Par exemple :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1626">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1627">La contrainte peut ensuite être appliquée aux itinéraires de la manière habituelle, en utilisant le nom spécifié lors de l’inscription du type de contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1627">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1628">Par exemple :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1628">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-1629">Informations de référence sur la génération d’URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1629">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1630">L’exemple suivant montre comment générer un lien vers une route selon un dictionnaire de valeurs de route et un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1630">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1631">Le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> généré à la fin de l’exemple précédent est `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1631">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1632">Le dictionnaire fournit les valeurs de route `operation` et `id` du modèle « Suivi de package de route », `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1632">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1633">Pour plus d’informations, consultez l’exemple de code dans la section [Utilisation du middleware de routage](#use-routing-middleware) ou l’[exemple d’application](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1633">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1634">Le deuxième paramètre pour le constructeur <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> est une collection de *valeurs ambiantes*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1634">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1635">Les valeurs ambiantes sont pratiques à utiliser, car elles limitent le nombre de valeurs qu’un développeur doit spécifier dans un contexte de requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1635">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1636">Les valeurs de route actuelles de la requête actuelle sont considérées comme des valeurs ambiantes pour la génération de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1636">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1637">Dans l’action `About` de `HomeController` d’une application ASP.NET Core MVC, vous n’avez pas besoin de spécifier la valeur de route du contrôleur pour créer un lien vers l’action `Index` : la valeur ambiante de `Home` est utilisée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1637">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1638">Les valeurs ambiantes qui ne correspondent pas à un paramètre sont ignorées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1638">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1639">Les valeurs ambiantes sont également ignorées quand une valeur explicitement fournie remplace la valeur ambiante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1639">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1640">La mise en correspondance se produit de gauche à droite dans l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1640">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1641">Les valeurs fournies explicitement mais qui n’ont pas de correspondance avec un segment de la route sont ajoutées à la chaîne de requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1641">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1642">Le tableau suivant présente le résultat en cas d’utilisation du modèle de routage `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1642">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1643">Valeurs ambiantes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1643">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1644">Valeurs explicites</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1644">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1645">Résultats</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1645">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1646">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1646">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1647">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1647">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1648">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1648">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1649">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1649">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1650">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1650">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1651">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1651">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1652">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1652">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1653">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1653">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1654">Si une route a une valeur par défaut qui ne correspond pas à un paramètre et que cette valeur est explicitement fournie, elle doit correspondre à la valeur par défaut :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1654">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1655">La génération de liens génère un lien pour cette route seulement quand les valeurs correspondantes pour `controller` et pour `action` sont fournies.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1655">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="128d2-1656">Segments complexes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1656">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="128d2-1657">Les segments complexes (par exemple, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) sont traités par la mise en correspondance des littéraux de droite à gauche de manière non gourmande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1657">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1658">Consultez [ce code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) pour obtenir une explication détaillée de la façon dont les segments complexes sont mis en correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1658">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="128d2-1659">[L’exemple de code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) n’est pas utilisé par ASP.NET Core, mais il fournit une bonne explication des segments complexes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="128d2-1659">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>

::: moniker-end
